class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.6.1.3.1.1" width="50%"><p>枚举值</p> </th> <th class="hljs-title class_">FG_PredictionMode</span></a></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>此枚举描述超帧预测算法模式。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 5.0.0(12)</p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.62.6.1.3.1.1" width="50%"><p>枚举值</p> </th> <th class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>内插模式，即通过第N-1帧真实渲染帧及第N帧真实渲染帧生成N-0.5帧预测帧。该模式适用于高渲染画质游戏和对运行平滑度要求高的游戏，如角色扮演游戏、竞速类游戏等。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>FG_PREDICTION_MODE_EXTRAPOLATION</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>外插模式，即通过N-1帧真实渲染帧及第N帧真实渲染帧生成N+0.5帧预测帧。该模式适用于对响应时延和操作跟手性要求高的游戏，如动作类游戏、射击类游戏等。</p> </td> </tr> class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="handle-button class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">enum</span> <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/_graphics_accelerate#gad7e5d2d235183dc0c6549331d6bc2932"><span class="hljs-title class_">OpenGTX_SceneID</span></a></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>此枚举描述OpenGTX算法的游戏场景类型。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 5.0.0(12)</p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.69.6.1.3.1.1" width="50%"><p>枚举值</p> </th> <th class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>LOADING</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>游戏场景类型为游戏加载中。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>PLAYING</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>游戏场景类型为游戏对局中。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>SPECTATOR</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>游戏场景类型为游戏观战中。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>DEATH</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>游戏场景类型为人物战斗准备中。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>HEAVY_LOAD</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>游戏场景类型为重负载。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>OTHERS_SCENE</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>游戏场景类型为其他场景。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 800px;"><h3 id="gaeff4735d18eb3086603ab6d04e7ad133" device-type="phone,tablet">OpenGTX_TempLevel<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cpp" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">enum</span> <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/_graphics_accelerate#gaeff4735d18eb3086603ab6d04e7ad133"><span class="hljs-title class_">OpenGTX_TempLevel</span></a></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>此枚举描述设备的温度级别。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 5.0.0(12)</p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.70.6.1.3.1.1" width="50%"><p>枚举值</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.70.6.1.3.1.2" width="50%"><p>描述</p> </th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>TEMP_LEVEL1</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>温度等级1。游戏可以保持当前配置。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>TEMP_LEVEL2</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>温度等级2。游戏应该减少不必要的服务，如减少后台更新。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>TEMP_LEVEL3</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>温度等级3。游戏应该停止非重点服务。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>TEMP_LEVEL4</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>温度等级4。游戏应该降低游戏效果。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>TEMP_LEVEL5</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>温度等级5。游戏要降低游戏场景配置，如帧分辨率、帧率、画质等。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>TEMP_LEVEL6</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>温度等级6。游戏应保持最低配置。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 146px;"><h2 id="section190079904093807" width="50%"><p>context</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>已创建的ABR上下文实例，即指向<a </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p> <p>函数执行结果状态。执行成功返回ABR_SUCCESS；失败返回具体错误码，具体失败错误码可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/_graphics_accelerate#ga86d5860f91dc4f1de6b381cd65389b9d">ABR_ErrorCode</a>。</p> </div> <div class="tiledSection" <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>销毁超帧输入输出图像实例，取消对应关联。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 5.0.0(12)</p> <p><strong>参数:</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>配置帧预测所需的参数信息，生成预测帧，该接口仅适配OpenGL ES图形API平台。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 5.0.0(12)</p> <p><strong>参数:</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p> <p>函数执行结果状态。执行成功返回FG_SUCCESS；失败返回具体错误码，具体失败错误码可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/_graphics_accelerate#ga394c554fc5d056d702180ee031ccee2c">FG_ErrorCode</a>。</p> </div> <div class="tiledSection" _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-dia-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-scss" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/_graphics_accelerate#ga68efbf5ff41faeb835f5587654c1e669">FG_ErrorCode</a> <span class="hljs-built_in">HMS_FG_SetDepthStencilYDirectionInverted_VK</span>(<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/_graphics_accelerate#ga4022ab63c2296d63dcf2c2df178508b7">FG_Context_VK</a>* context, bool inverted )</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>设置颜色缓冲区相对深度模板缓冲区是否存在y轴翻转的标志位，可选调用，未调用则默认无翻转。该接口仅适配Vulkan图形API平台。 如果存在翻转但没有将inverted设置为true，可能导致预测帧效果异常。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 5.0.0(12)</p> <p><strong>参数:</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.111.7.1.3.1.1" width="50%"><p>名称</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.111.7.1.3.1.2" width="50%"><p>描述</p> </th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>context</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>已创建的超帧上下文实例，即指向<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/_graphics_accelerate#ga4022ab63c2296d63dcf2c2df178508b7">FG_Context_VK</a>对象的指针，不允许为空。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>inverted</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>颜色缓冲区相对深度模板缓冲区是否存在y轴翻转的标志位。</p> <p>true : 颜色缓冲区相对深度模板缓冲区基于y轴翻转180°；</p> <p>false : 颜色缓冲区相对深度模板缓冲区无翻转。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p> <p>函数执行结果状态。执行成功返回FG_SUCCESS；失败返回具体错误码，具体失败错误码可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/_graphics_accelerate#ga394c554fc5d056d702180ee031ccee2c">FG_ErrorCode</a>。</p> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 772px;"><h3 id="gaafa490d4377cc5babbc0ac0f4f7b78a7" device-type="phone,tablet">HMS_FG_SetImageFormat_GLES()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>设置真实渲染帧颜色缓冲区和预测帧缓冲区的图像格式，可选调用，未调用则模式默认设置为FG_FORMAT_R8G8B8A8_UNORM。该接口仅适配OpenGL ES图形API平台。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 5.0.0(12)</p> <p><strong>参数:</strong></p>  <div <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>设置超帧集成信息，该接口仅适配OpenGL ES图形API平台。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 5.1.0(18)</p> <p><strong>参数:</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="linenums"><li><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/_graphics_accelerate#ga97deebd9adf3e19947ec5b4615fa1d9c">OpenGTX_ErrorCode</a> <span <p>设置OpenGTX运行所需的网络延迟信息。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 5.0.0(12)</p> <p><strong>参数:</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.135.7.1.3.1.1" width="50%"><p>名称</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.135.7.1.3.1.2" width="50%"><p>描述</p> </th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>context</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>已创建的OpenGTX上下文实例，即指向<a class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>networkInfo</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>网络信息，即指向OpenGTX网络信息结构体<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/_open_g_t_x___network_info">OpenGTX_NetworkInfo</a>的指针；非空，否则返回失败。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p> <p>函数执行结果状态。执行成功返回OPENGTX_SUCCESS；失败返回具体错误码，具体失败错误码可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/_graphics_accelerate#gaa2c657ed21a175b099bea0ed2491cc34">OpenGTX_ErrorCode</a>。</p> </div> <div class="tiledSection"
